[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreasonable[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[95msize[0m[39m to limit excessive computation[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m:    private static final Pattern FRACTION_FORMAT =[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"[0m[32m([0m[32m[[0m[32m+-[0m[32m][0m[32m)[0m[32m?[0m[32m([0m[32m\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m0,20[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m0,20[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m?[0m[32m)[0m[32m "[0m[39m +[0m             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-text-m[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/csv/CellFormatter.jav[0m[1;92ma:67[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m75[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:        for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, denomLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - 1d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; i > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i--[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:            for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i2 = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, denomLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - 1d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; i2 >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i2--[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mminVal >= [0m[1;35mMath.abs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi2 [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi - decPart[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:                    currDenom = i;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:                    currNum = i2;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:                    minVal = [0m[1;35mMath.abs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m i2 [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m i - decPart[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mCellFormatter.format[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method uses a brute-force nested loop over all [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumerator/denominator pairs up to `[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^denomLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`. Since `denomLength` can be [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mup to [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom the regex group[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the loops potentially iterate [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m20[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m times, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcausing the parser to hang or time out.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The regex limits the *pattern* size but does not bound the *computation* [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minduced by that size. We must re-introduce a practical cap on `denomLength` to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoid pathological runtime.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy Overview[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduce a small constant `MAX_DENOM_LENGTH` [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to clamp or bail out [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore entering the expensive loops.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If the matched `[0m[1;35mdenomFormat.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` exceeds `MAX_DENOM_LENGTH`, skip [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfraction formatting altogether and return the original cell. This preserves [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectness for typical cases but prevents runaway computation on pathological [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Does not modify fuzzing harness or tests.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Keeps existing parsing logic intact for denominators up to the cap.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Avoids quadratic blow-up without introducing heavy new dependencies or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithms.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Is simple to review and maintain.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `CellFormatter.java`, add at the top of the class [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbelow existing static [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfields[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Maximum number of digits allowed in the denominator to keep formatting [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcost bounded[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static final int MAX_DENOM_FORMAT_DIGITS = [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In `[0m[1;35mformat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, locate the block after extracting `denomFormat`:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String denomFormat = [0m[1;35mfractionFormatMatcher.group[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m5[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int denomLength = [0m[1;35mdenomFormat.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Immediately after computing `denomLength`, insert a guard:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenomLength > MAX_DENOM_FORMAT_DIGITS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Input requests too large a denominator — skip formatting to avoid [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexcessive computation[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return cell;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Leave the subsequent brute-force loops [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m67[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m75[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m unchanged. They now only[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrun when the denominator length is ≤ [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m, capping the worst-case inner iterations at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m1e6[0m[39m.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Functionality[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Common cases with small denominators [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"1/2"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"3/4"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"12/100"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are still [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatted correctly.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fallback: any format request with >[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m digits of denominator will simply be left[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munformatted, avoiding the performance hazard.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do *not* alter any other parsing or fuzzing logic, so all existing tests [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand the harness will continue to operate unchanged.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side Effect: Very large fraction formats will no longer be converted to mixed [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor simplified fraction representations. Instead, the raw cell string is returned.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: Document this limitation in the Javadoc comment above [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CellFormatter`, indicating that denominator formatting is capped to [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MAX_DENOM_FORMAT_DIGITS` for performance reasons.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If future users require precise formatting of larger denominators, they can [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mopt into a specialized, efficient rational-approximation implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., via [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinued fractions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in a separate utility.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References and Similar Patterns[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The class comment already mentions “limits integer precision … to a reasonable[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize.” This patch enforces that principle at runtime.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No existing code in Tika parses user-specified precision in a way that leaks [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto unbounded loops; this change brings `CellFormatter` in line with other [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumeric-formatting utilities in Tika that guard against runaway patterns.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. No Additional File Retrieval Needed[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All required context is present in `CellFormatter.java`. No changes to harness[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor other files are necessary.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No test code modifications.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
